| <span data-ttu-id="075f3-713">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="075f3-713">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="075f3-714">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="075f3-714">Value</span></span> |
